// client/src/pages/operate/RunTracePage.tsx
//
// ============================================================
// EMBEDDED-MODE RECURSION GUARD (INVARIANT ƒ?" do not remove)
// ============================================================
// When `embedded === true` this page is rendered inside an <iframe> launched
// by <RunTraceModal>. Every affordance that could open ANOTHER RunTraceModal
// or another iframe-embedded run-trace MUST be suppressed:
//
//   1. Run-id references render as plain text or copy-chip, NOT as
//      <RunTraceModal> triggers.
//   2. Cross-run links (parent/child run pointers) become:
//        <a href="/run-trace/:otherId" target="_top">
//      NOT modal launches. Using target="_top" keeps navigation in the top
//      window so the user exits the iframe rather than spawning a nested one.
//   3. The placeholder renderer (and, in C5b, <RunTraceEventRenderer>)
//      receives `embedded` as a prop and disables "open in modal" affordances.
//
// Any future feature that adds a run-id link or "open" button inside this
// page MUST check the `embedded` flag and apply the same suppression.
// ============================================================

import { useEffect, useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';
import { useParams, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import api from '../../lib/api';
import { User } from '../../lib/auth';
import { AGENT_RUN_STATUS, isTerminalRunStatus } from '../../lib/runStatus';
import { useSocketRoom } from '../../hooks/useSocket';
import { parseEmbeddedFlag } from '../../lib/runTraceEmbeddedPure';
import { WorkspaceBadge } from '../../components/WorkspaceBadge';
import { PageShell } from '../../components/PageShell';
import type { RunDetail } from '../../components/runs/RunTraceView';
import { RunTraceEventRenderer } from './components/RunTraceEventRenderer';

// ƒ"?ƒ"? IEE progress polling (ported from RunTraceViewerPage) ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?

interface IeeProgress {
  ieeRunId: string;
  status: string;
  stepCount: number;
  heartbeatAgeSeconds: number | null;
  startedAt: string | null;
  failureReason: string | null;
}

const POLL_BACKOFF_SCHEDULE_MS = [3_000, 5_000, 10_000] as const;
const POLL_MAX_DURATION_MS = 15 * 60 * 1_000; // 15 minutes


// ƒ"?ƒ"? RunTracePage ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?

export default function RunTracePage({ user: _user }: { user: User }) {
  const { id: runId } = useParams<{ id: string }>();
  const location = useLocation();

  // Read embedded flag ONCE on mount ƒ?" not reactive (per spec ¶õ4.3).
  // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  const embedded = useRef(parseEmbeddedFlag(location.search)).current;

  const [run, setRun] = useState<RunDetail | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const [chainRuns, setChainRuns] = useState<Array<{
    id: string; agentName: string; isSubAgent: boolean; runSource: string;
    status: string; startedAt: string | null; completedAt: string | null;
    durationMs: number | null; totalTokens: number | null;
  }>>([]);

  const [ieeProgress, setIeeProgress] = useState<IeeProgress | null>(null);

  // ƒ"?ƒ"? Data fetch ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?

  const refreshRun = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!runId) return;
    try {
      const { data } = await api.get(`/api/agent-runs/${runId}`);
      setRun(data);
    } catch {
      // Silent ƒ?" the initial load handles the error state.
    }
  }, [runId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!runId) return;
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    api.get(`/api/agent-runs/${runId}`)
      .then(({ data }) => setRun(data))
      .catch((err) => setError(err.response?.data?.error ?? 'Failed to load run'))
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
    api.get(`/api/agent-runs/${runId}/chain`)
      .then(({ data }) => setChainRuns(data.runs ?? []))
      .catch(() => setChainRuns([]));
  }, [runId]);

  // ƒ"?ƒ"? WebSocket room subscription (ported from RunTraceViewerPage) ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?

  useSocketRoom(
    'agent-run',
    runId ?? null,
    {
      'agent:run:delegated': refreshRun,
      'agent:run:completed': refreshRun,
      'agent:run:failed': refreshRun,
    },
    refreshRun,
  );

  // ƒ"?ƒ"? IEE Phase 0 ƒ?" delegated run progress polling ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?ƒ"?

  const ieeRunId = run?.status === AGENT_RUN_STATUS.DELEGATED
    ? (run?.ieeRunId ?? null)
    : null;

  // subaccountId may arrive via query param (promoted by C8 redirect from the
  // old /admin/subaccounts/:id/runs/:runId path).
  const subaccountIdFromQuery = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get('subaccountId');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!ieeRunId) {
      setIeeProgress(null);
      return;
    }
    let cancelled = false;
    let timer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null;
    let lastStepCount = -1;
    let lastStatus = '';
    let backoffIdx = 0;
    const startedAt = Date.now();
    const subaccountParam = subaccountIdFromQuery
      ? `?subaccountId=${encodeURIComponent(subaccountIdFromQuery)}`
      : '';

    const clearTimer = () => {
      if (timer) clearTimeout(timer);
      timer = null;
    };

    const scheduleNext = () => {
      if (cancelled) return;
      if (document.visibilityState !== 'visible') return;
      if (Date.now() - startedAt >= POLL_MAX_DURATION_MS) return;
      const delay = POLL_BACKOFF_SCHEDULE_MS[
        Math.min(backoffIdx, POLL_BACKOFF_SCHEDULE_MS.length - 1)
      ];
      timer = setTimeout(fetchProgress, delay);
    };

    const fetchProgress = async () => {
      if (cancelled) return;
      if (document.visibilityState !== 'visible') return;
      try {
        const { data } = await api.get(
          `/api/iee/runs/${ieeRunId}/progress${subaccountParam}`,
        );
        if (cancelled) return;
        setIeeProgress(data);
        if (['completed', 'failed', 'cancelled'].includes(data?.status)) {
          cancelled = true;
          clearTimer();
          refreshRun();
          return;
        }
        const progressed =
          typeof data?.stepCount === 'number' &&
          (data.stepCount !== lastStepCount || data.status !== lastStatus);
        if (progressed) {
          backoffIdx = 0;
          lastStepCount = typeof data.stepCount === 'number' ? data.stepCount : lastStepCount;
          lastStatus = typeof data.status === 'string' ? data.status : lastStatus;
        } else {
          backoffIdx = Math.min(backoffIdx + 1, POLL_BACKOFF_SCHEDULE_MS.length - 1);
        }
      } catch {
        backoffIdx = Math.min(backoffIdx + 1, POLL_BACKOFF_SCHEDULE_MS.length - 1);
      }
      scheduleNext();
    };

At line:1 char:1
+ [Console]::OutputEncoding=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8;
+ ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
    + CategoryInfo          : InvalidOperation: (:) [], RuntimeException
    + FullyQualifiedErrorId : PropertySetterNotSupportedInConstrainedLanguage
 

codex
1. **§6.1/§6.2/§6.3/§6.4 and §8, critical — RLS setting name is wrong.**  
   Policies use `current_setting('app.current_organisation_id')`, but the repo manifest documents `app.organisation_id`. This will fail closed or bypass intended context depending on setup.  
   **Fix:** change all new policies to the repo’s canonical setting and match existing RLS policy shape.

2. **§6.5 and §5, critical — `iee_artifacts` contract does not match the repo.**  
   Spec says existing `iee_artifacts` has `run_id`, but the actual schema has `iee_run_id` plus metadata, and `agent_runs` has `ieeRunId`. The four-tuple lineage cannot be implemented as written.  
   **Fix:** define the join path explicitly: `agent_runs.id -> agent_runs.iee_run_id -> iee_artifacts.iee_run_id`, or add a real `agent_run_id`/`run_id` column with FK and index.

3. **§9/§11.1/§12.4, critical — `last_event_seq` is not a safe global replay watermark.**  
   `agent_execution_events.sequence_number` is scoped per run. A single `last_event_seq` per agent or rollup will drop or misorder events from concurrent runs.  
   **Fix:** use `(run_id, sequence_number)` processed markers, or add/use a globally monotonic event ordering column. Do not watermark multi-run projections with run-local sequence alone.

4. **§7.5/§11.1, critical — working-time rollup idempotency breaks with concurrent runs.**  
   `agent_working_time_rollups.last_event_seq` has the same per-run sequence problem, while §7.5 explicitly allows concurrent runs and summed intervals.  
   **Fix:** make rollup application idempotent by `event_id`/processed-event ledger or per-run watermarks, then aggregate into buckets.

5. **§11.7 vs §12.3, critical — stale running state has contradictory outcomes.**  
   §12.3 says delayed events/heartbeat staleness enter `degraded`; §11.7 says latest event age >60s while running flips to `failed` or `idle`. That changes uncertainty into terminal failure without a failure event.  
   **Fix:** reserve `failed` for explicit terminal/failure signals. Use `degraded` for stale telemetry, with a separate hard timeout only if backed by an existing terminal mechanism.

6. **§12.3/§13.4, important — client disconnect is mixed into server-derived presence.**  
   `orchestration_disconnected` depends on a client’s stream connection, but `AgentPresenceState` is supposed to be server-derived and shared by all surfaces. One tab disconnecting cannot mutate canonical agent presence.  
   **Fix:** split local transport health from canonical presence. Keep reconnect banners client-local; only server-observed stream/worker failures affect `agent_presence_projections`.

7. **§5 Phase 5, important — run-trace file inventory is stale.**  
   Spec names `client/src/pages/build/RunTracePage.tsx`, but the repo has `client/src/pages/operate/RunTracePage.tsx`, with rendering through `RunTraceEventRenderer`/run-trace components.  
   **Fix:** update inventory and implementation target to the actual operate page and event renderer/component path.

8. **§4 Phase 3 / §5 Phase 3, important — Home widget plan does not fit `MetricCard`.**  
   The spec says “replace existing Active Agents `MetricCard` body”, but `MetricCard` has fixed `label/value/sub/icon` props and no children/body slot. Inventory does not include modifying `MetricCard`.  
   **Fix:** either modify `MetricCard` to accept rich children and list it as `M`, or replace the Active Agents tile with a dedicated widget/card component in `HomePage`.

9. **§8, important — permission names do not match the codebase.**  
   Spec uses `AGENT_VIEW`, `AGENT_OBSERVATIONS_PIN`, and `AGENT_PRESENCE_STREAM_SUBSCRIBE`; current permissions use names like `ORG_PERMISSIONS.AGENTS_VIEW`.  
   **Fix:** name exact permission constants/files to modify, or state that new `ORG_PERMISSIONS.*` keys will be added in `server/lib/permissions.ts`.

10. **§6.1/§7.3/§11.1, important — observation idempotency is too coarse.**  
   `UNIQUE(event_id, observation_type)` allows only one `learned` or `detected` observation per event, which conflicts with multi-fact step outputs.  
   **Fix:** add an explicit `idempotency_key` or unique tuple including `source_kind/source_id/content_hash`, while allowing multiple observations of the same type per event.

11. **§6.1, important — append-only observation claim lacks a DB mechanism.**  
   The spec says rows are immutable but enforces this only through service discipline. That is load-bearing for provenance and correction semantics.  
   **Fix:** add DB-level protection compatible with maintenance, such as revoking `UPDATE/DELETE` from the app role or an immutability trigger with a documented maintenance bypass.

12. **§7.5, important — billable boundary for external calls is ambiguous.**  
   “Active LLM call or tool call” is included, but “External API in flight” is excluded. Many tool calls are external API calls.  
   **Fix:** define the accounting boundary mechanically: bill local/container/LLM execution time, exclude passive wait/backoff after the request leaves the worker, and specify the exact event pairs emitted for each interval.

13. **§15.1 vs §1.3/§4, important — Phase 1 dependency is unresolved but later phases depend on it.**  
   The spec says Phase 1 can slip with graceful degradation, but Phase 5 requires the locked Knowledge Files deep-link/version contract and §4 assumes Phase 1 lands first.  
   **Fix:** split “Overview degraded without Phase 1” from “lineage chips blocked until Phase 1 contract exists,” and make Phase 5 explicitly dependent on that contract.

14. **§14.2/§5 Phase 6, minor — file inventory includes out-of-repo deliverables.**  
   “Sales decks / product copy / blog drafts” are listed as modified but “outside the repo.” That breaks the inventory lock as an implementation checklist.  
   **Fix:** move external sweep to acceptance notes, and keep §5 inventory to repo files only.

1. **§6.1/§6.2/§6.3/§6.4 and §8, critical — RLS setting name is wrong.**  
   Policies use `current_setting('app.current_organisation_id')`, but the repo manifest documents `app.organisation_id`. This will fail closed or bypass intended context depending on setup.  
   **Fix:** change all new policies to the repo’s canonical setting and match existing RLS policy shape.

2. **§6.5 and §5, critical — `iee_artifacts` contract does not match the repo.**  
   Spec says existing `iee_artifacts` has `run_id`, but the actual schema has `iee_run_id` plus metadata, and `agent_runs` has `ieeRunId`. The four-tuple lineage cannot be implemented as written.  
   **Fix:** define the join path explicitly: `agent_runs.id -> agent_runs.iee_run_id -> iee_artifacts.iee_run_id`, or add a real `agent_run_id`/`run_id` column with FK and index.

3. **§9/§11.1/§12.4, critical — `last_event_seq` is not a safe global replay watermark.**  
   `agent_execution_events.sequence_number` is scoped per run. A single `last_event_seq` per agent or rollup will drop or misorder events from concurrent runs.  
   **Fix:** use `(run_id, sequence_number)` processed markers, or add/use a globally monotonic event ordering column. Do not watermark multi-run projections with run-local sequence alone.

4. **§7.5/§11.1, critical — working-time rollup idempotency breaks with concurrent runs.**  
   `agent_working_time_rollups.last_event_seq` has the same per-run sequence problem, while §7.5 explicitly allows concurrent runs and summed intervals.  
   **Fix:** make rollup application idempotent by `event_id`/processed-event ledger or per-run watermarks, then aggregate into buckets.

5. **§11.7 vs §12.3, critical — stale running state has contradictory outcomes.**
